Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-29 17:42:20]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

		, birth_place
		, religion
		, race
		, designation
        , employer_id
		, home_phone
		, malaysia_phone
		, office_phone
		, local_address
        , home_address
        , home_country
		, email
		, office_email
		, username
        , pswd
		, is_admin
        , access_level
		, chat_id
		, dept_id
		, reporting_to_id
		, allow_add
        , allow_approve
        , allow_verify
        , allow_contract_approve
		, allow_contract_create
		, allow_contract_view_all
		, allow_contract_access
		, general_skills
        , specific_skills
        , date_format(work_start_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_start_date
        , date_format(work_end_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_end_date
        , salary
        , date_format(ep_valid_till,'%d-%m-%Y') as ep_valid_till
        , notice_period_id
		, spouse_name
		, spouse_occupation
		, date_format(marriage_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as marriage_date
		, spouse_ic
		, spouse_company
		, spouse_company_address
		, no_of_children
		, emergency_person
		, emergency_relation
		, emergency_address
		, emergency_phone
		, bank_acc_name
		, bank_acc_ic
		, bank_name
		, bank_account_no
		, accessible_ctg
		, super_admin
		, is_active
		, concat('http://127.0.0.1/mspdoc_bare/services/files/', 'photos/',id,'.jpeg') as profile_pic
		, date_format(leaving_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as leaving_date
		, leaving_reason
		, created_by
        , (select employer_name from cms_master_employer where cms_master_employer.id = cms_employees.employer_id) as employer_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.dept_id) as dept_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.notice_period_id) as notice_period
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.access_level) as access_level_name

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-29 17:45:25]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

        , employer_id
		, home_phone
		, malaysia_phone
		, office_phone
		, local_address
        , home_address

		, is_admin
        , access_level

		, reporting_to_id
		, allow_add

        , allow_verify
        , allow_contract_approve
		, allow_contract_create
		, allow_contract_view_all
		, allow_contract_access
		, general_skills
        , specific_skills
        , date_format(work_start_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_start_date
        , date_format(work_end_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_end_date
        , salary
        , date_format(ep_valid_till,'%d-%m-%Y') as ep_valid_till
        , notice_period_id
		, spouse_name
		, spouse_occupation
		, date_format(marriage_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as marriage_date
		, spouse_ic

		, date_format(leaving_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as leaving_date
		, leaving_reason
		, created_by
        , (select employer_name from cms_master_employer where cms_master_employer.id = cms_employees.employer_id) as employer_name

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-29 17:46:50]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

		, office_phone

        , home_address
        , home_country

		, is_admin

        , allow_contract_approve
		, allow_contract_create
		, allow_contract_view_all
		, allow_contract_access
		, general_skills
        , specific_skills
        , date_format(work_start_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_start_date
        , date_format(work_end_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_end_date
        , salary
        , date_format(ep_valid_till,'%d-%m-%Y') as ep_valid_till
        , notice_period_id
		, spouse_name
		, spouse_occupation
		, date_format(marriage_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as marriage_date

		, date_format(leaving_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as leaving_date
		, leaving_reason
		, created_by
        , (select employer_name from cms_master_employer where cms_master_employer.id = cms_employees.employer_id) as employer_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.dept_id) as dept_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.notice_period_id) as notice_period

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-29 17:51:05]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id

                         UNION ALL

                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id

				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

		, reporting_to_id

        , allow_contract_approve
		, allow_contract_create
		, allow_contract_view_all
		, allow_contract_access
		, general_skills
        , specific_skills
        , date_format(work_start_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_start_date
        , date_format(work_end_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_end_date
        , salary
        , date_format(ep_valid_till,'%d-%m-%Y') as ep_valid_till
        , notice_period_id
		, spouse_name
		, spouse_occupation
		, date_format(marriage_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as marriage_date

		, leaving_reason
		, created_by
        , (select employer_name from cms_master_employer where cms_master_employer.id = cms_employees.employer_id) as employer_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.dept_id) as dept_name

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-29 17:52:32]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

		, nationality
		, birth_place
		, religion
		, race
		, designation
        , employer_id
		, home_phone
		, malaysia_phone
		, office_phone
		, local_address
        , home_address
        , home_country
		, email
		, office_email
		, username
        , pswd
		, is_admin
        , access_level
		, chat_id
		, dept_id
		, reporting_to_id
		, allow_add
        , allow_approve
        , allow_verify
        , allow_contract_approve
		, allow_contract_create
		, allow_contract_view_all
		, allow_contract_access
		, general_skills
        , specific_skills
        , date_format(work_start_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_start_date
        , date_format(work_end_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_end_date
        , salary
        , date_format(ep_valid_till,'%d-%m-%Y') as ep_valid_till
        , notice_period_id
		, spouse_name
		, spouse_occupation
		, date_format(marriage_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as marriage_date
		, spouse_ic
		, spouse_company
		, spouse_company_address
		, no_of_children
		, emergency_person
		, emergency_relation
		, emergency_address
		, emergency_phone
		, bank_acc_name
		, bank_acc_ic
		, bank_name
		, bank_account_no
		, accessible_ctg
		, super_admin
		, is_active
		, concat('http://127.0.0.1/mspdoc_bare/services/files/', 'photos/',id,'.jpeg') as profile_pic
		, date_format(leaving_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as leaving_date
		, leaving_reason
		, created_by
        , (select employer_name from cms_master_employer where cms_master_employer.id = cms_employees.employer_id) as employer_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.dept_id) as dept_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.notice_period_id) as notice_period
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.access_level) as access_level_name

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-29 17:53:00]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

		, birth_place
		, religion
		, race
		, designation
        , employer_id
		, home_phone
		, malaysia_phone
		, office_phone
		, local_address
        , home_address
        , home_country
		, email
		, office_email
		, username
        , pswd
		, is_admin
        , access_level
		, chat_id
		, dept_id
		, reporting_to_id
		, allow_add
        , allow_approve
        , allow_verify
        , allow_contract_approve
		, allow_contract_create
		, allow_contract_view_all
		, allow_contract_access
		, general_skills
        , specific_skills
        , date_format(work_start_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_start_date
        , date_format(work_end_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_end_date
        , salary
        , date_format(ep_valid_till,'%d-%m-%Y') as ep_valid_till
        , notice_period_id
		, spouse_name
		, spouse_occupation
		, date_format(marriage_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as marriage_date
		, spouse_ic
		, spouse_company
		, spouse_company_address
		, no_of_children
		, emergency_person
		, emergency_relation
		, emergency_address

		, bank_account_no

		, super_admin
		, is_active
		, concat('http://127.0.0.1/mspdoc_bare/services/files/', 'photos/',id,'.jpeg') as profile_pic
		, date_format(leaving_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as leaving_date
		, leaving_reason
		, created_by
        , (select employer_name from cms_master_employer where cms_master_employer.id = cms_employees.employer_id) as employer_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.dept_id) as dept_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.notice_period_id) as notice_period

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-29 17:53:25]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

 Param Details :

[2018-12-29 17:55:34]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT 
        id
        , employee_no
        , name
        , photoname
		, ic_passport
		, sex_id
		, age
		, date_format(dob,'%d-%m-%Y') as dob
		, nationality
		, birth_place
		, religion
		, race
		, designation
        , employer_id
		, home_phone
		, malaysia_phone
		, office_phone
		, local_address
        , home_address
        , home_country
		, email
		, office_email
		, username
        , pswd
		, is_admin
        , access_level
		, chat_id
		, dept_id
		, reporting_to_id
		, allow_add
        , allow_approve
        , allow_verify
        , allow_contract_approve
		, allow_contract_create
		, allow_contract_view_all
		, allow_contract_access
		, general_skills
        , specific_skills
        , date_format(work_start_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_start_date
        , date_format(work_end_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_end_date
        , salary
        , date_format(ep_valid_till,'%d-%m-%Y') as ep_valid_till
        , notice_period_id
		, spouse_name
		, spouse_occupation
		, date_format(marriage_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as marriage_date
		, spouse_ic
		, spouse_company
		, spouse_company_address
		, no_of_children
		, emergency_person
		, emergency_relation
		, emergency_address
		, emergency_phone
		, bank_acc_name
		, bank_acc_ic
		, bank_name
		, bank_account_no
		, accessible_ctg
		, super_admin
		, is_active
		, concat('http://127.0.0.1/mspdoc_bare/services/files/', 'photos/',id,'.jpeg') as profile_pic
		, date_format(leaving_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as leaving_date
		, leaving_reason
		, created_by
        , (select employer_name from cms_master_employer where cms_master_employer.id = cms_employees.employer_id) as employer_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.dept_id) as dept_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.notice_period_id) as notice_period
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.access_level) as access_level_name
         FROM cms_employees WHERE id = 15

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-29 18:02:48]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: get_document_archiving_list 
 Param Details :

[2018-12-29 18:03:05]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

						, is_admin, initial_pswd

		                , accessible_ctg
						, malaysia_phone
						, concat('http://127.0.0.1/mspdoc_bare/services/files/', 'photos/',id,'.jpeg') as profile_pic
		                , super_admin  FROM cms_employees

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

		, leaving_reason

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: get_document_archiving_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","type_id":"","status_id":"","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-12-29 18:07:44]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_document_archiving.attachment

                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving

                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: get_document_archiving_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","type_id":"","status_id":"","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-12-29 18:36:38]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by

				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

        , employer_id
		, home_phone
		, malaysia_phone
		, office_phone
		, local_address
        , home_address
        , home_country
		, email
		, office_email
		, username
        , pswd
		, is_admin
        , access_level
		, chat_id
		, dept_id
		, reporting_to_id
		, allow_add
        , allow_approve
        , allow_verify
        , allow_contract_approve
		, allow_contract_create
		, allow_contract_view_all
		, allow_contract_access
		, general_skills
        , specific_skills
        , date_format(work_start_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_start_date
        , date_format(work_end_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as work_end_date
        , salary
        , date_format(ep_valid_till,'%d-%m-%Y') as ep_valid_till

		, date_format(marriage_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as marriage_date

		, date_format(leaving_date,'%d-%m-%Y') as leaving_date
		, leaving_reason
		, created_by
        , (select employer_name from cms_master_employer where cms_master_employer.id = cms_employees.employer_id) as employer_name
        , (select descr from cms_master_list where cms_master_list.id = cms_employees.dept_id) as dept_name

Function Details: db_execute_custom_sql
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_appt_pic.id,cms_appt_pic.name,cms_appt_pic.email, cms_clients.name as company_name
                        FROM cms_appt_pic INNER JOIN cms_clients ON cms_appt_pic.client = cms_clients.id
                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

Function Details: get_document_archiving_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","type_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-12-29 18:50:38]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-12-29 20:21:57]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, cms_document_archiving.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.notes
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, cms_document_archiving.status_id
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name		
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

                        WHERE cms_appt_pic.created_by = 15 
                         UNION ALL
                        SELECT cms_employees.id, cms_employees.name, cms_employees.office_email as email,
                        cms_master_employer.employer_name  as company_name
                        FROM
                        cms_employees INNER JOIN cms_master_employer ON cms_employees.employer_id = cms_master_employer.id
                        WHERE cms_employees.is_active = 1

[2018-12-29 23:37:55]
Function Details: get_outbound_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-12-29 23:37:55]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_outbound_document.outbound_no
				, cms_outbound_document.outbound_date
				, cms_outbound_document.client_id
				, cms_outbound_document.employer_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_outbound_document.attention_to
				, cms_outbound_document.email_content
				, cms_outbound_document.email
				, cms_outbound_document.attachment
				, cms_outbound_document.remarks
				, cms_outbound_document.amount
				, cms_outbound_document.notes
				, cms_outbound_document.approvals
				, cms_outbound_document.status_id
				, cms_outbound_document.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_outbound_document.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_outbound_document.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_outbound_document
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_outbound_document.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_outbound_document.created_by) AND cms_outbound_document.is_active in(1) ORDER BY outbound_no DESC limit 0,10
